  I just made minor changes for self-understanding. I don't claim authority of any class.

Data type for a code segment. Can be a regular segment, block of code
segments, a par statement (cobegin/coend) as well as while loops and if
statements.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2956" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Seg"></a><a id="2961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2961" class="Datatype">Seg</a> <a id="2965" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2967" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2971" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="LTL._==n_"></a><a id="4625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4625" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==n_</a>        <a id="4638" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4640" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4641" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4643" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4645" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1098" class="Datatype">NVar</a><a id="4649" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4651" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4653" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4654" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4654" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="4656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4658" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="4659" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4661" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4663" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4051" class="Datatype">LTL</a>     <a id="4671" class="Comment">-- Nat variable x has the value n</a>
  <a id="LTL._==b_"></a><a id="4707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4707" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==b_</a>        <a id="4720" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4722" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4723" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4725" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1198" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4731" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4733" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4735" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4736" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4738" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4740" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1198" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4744" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4746" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4748" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4051" class="Datatype">LTL</a>  <a id="4753" class="Comment">-- Bool variable x has the value of y</a>
  <a id="LTL.isTrue"></a><a id="4793" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4793" class="InductiveConstructor">isTrue</a>       <a id="4806" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4808" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4809" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4811" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1198" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4817" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4819" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4051" class="Datatype">LTL</a>               <a id="4839" class="Comment">-- Variable x has the value -- true</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## The LTL-rule data type

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6762" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="LTLRule"></a><a id="6767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6767" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a> <a id="6775" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6777" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6781" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₁"></a><a id="6789" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6789" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₁</a>   <a id="6796" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4051" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6802" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6767" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6819" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on first element</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₂"></a><a id="6857" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6857" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₂</a>   <a id="6864" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6866" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4051" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6870" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6872" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6767" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6887" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on second element</a>

## Propositional logic representation

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10438" class="Comment">-- Representation of propositional logic</a>
<a id="10479" class="Comment">-- data Props : Set where</a>
<a id="10505" class="Comment">--   T ⊥         : Props</a>
<a id="10530" class="Comment">--   _∧_ _∨_ _⇒_ : Props → Props → Props</a>
<a id="10571" class="Comment">--   p&#39;          : ℕ → Props</a>
<a id="10600" class="Comment">--   ~_          : Props → Props</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Translator

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10673" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Translator"></a><a id="10680" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#10680" class="Module">Translator</a> <a id="10691" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Translator for concurrent programs. Translates program representations into
transition relations (TransRel). The relations keep track of the LTL-formulas
related to the program statements of the programs.

### Actions

Data type for actions, reference to what happened when translating the program

### Hoare-style Triples

Represents transition relations, < pre > action < post >, where pre is the
precondition of the program statement, action the reference to the type of
program statement, and post the postcondition of the statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12049" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="TransRel"></a><a id="12054" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12054" class="Datatype">TransRel</a> <a id="12063" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12065" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="12069" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="TransRel.&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;"></a><a id="12077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12077" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;</a> <a id="12085" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12087" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12088" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="12091" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12093" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4051" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12096" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12098" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12100" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11025" class="Datatype">Action</a> <a id="12107" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12109" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12110" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="12113" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12115" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4051" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12118" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12120" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12122" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12054" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>  <a id="12132" class="Comment">-- Hoare-style Triple</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translates a program statement into the corresponding `TransRel`.
  * `l`: Program label of the program statement.
  * `Stm`: The program statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="transStm"></a><a id="12330" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12330" class="Function">transStm</a> <a id="12339" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12341" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#981" class="Datatype">Label</a> <a id="12347" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2481" class="Datatype">Stm</a> <a id="12353" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12355" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12054" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

Flattens a list of lists into a single list.

Converts a list of segments and a label, representing a single block segment,
into a list of `TransRel`. The result contains the representation of the program
flow.

* `p`: Label of the parent segment.
* `List Seg`: List of all child segments.

Converts a list of segments into a single `LTL`. The list represents all child
segments initiated by a parent `par` segment. The result is an `LTL` used as a
precondition in order to allow the parent segment to be considered executed.

Helper function for translate that uses different translation approaches
depending on the type of segment to be translated.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15262" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="15266" class="Keyword">TERMINATING</a> <a id="15278" class="Symbol">#-}</a> <a id="15282" class="Comment">-- used to guarantee that there is no infinite looping</a>

  <a id="16751" class="Comment">-- Translate the if statement</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translate function that takes a program and returns a list of TransRel.
The list consists of two parts, first the statement specific translations,
the second the program flow relations between the segments.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="translate"></a><a id="17015" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#17015" class="Function">translate</a> <a id="17025" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3819" class="Record">Prog</a> <a id="17032" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17034" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.List.html#80" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="17039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12054" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

## Rules to construct proofs

Contains rules to use when construction proofs. Also has functions to check if
rules are used legally. Used in ProofChecker

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17304" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Rules"></a><a id="17311" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#17311" class="Module">Rules</a> <a id="17317" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Data type for program rules, indexed with rule and `LTL`. Specifically for
proof-steps regarding the programs

                                             <a id="18208" class="Comment">-- control progression</a>
